=        hints        =
=======================
1) any comments allowed in this file
2) * means null value
3) 0 means zero-weighted value
4) no rows allowed between #matrix definition and matrix
5) any spaces allowed
6) in non-oriented graphs only top-right values handled
7) top-left - down-right diagonal line always must be null (* filled)
